## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 71 page(s) - 71 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<div class="cookie-text">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.cookie-text
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.cookie-text')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://bayern.de/
- https://bayern.de/erklaerung-zur-barrierefreiheit/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/apps-messenger-rss/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/broschueren/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/buergerbeauftragter/
- *...and 66 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 70 page(s) - 70 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html

```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a
```

**How to Replicate**:

#### Pattern 12: Affects 70 page(s) - 70 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**Issue**: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="openNav"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="openNav"]')`

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://bayern.de/

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="/eu-finanzen-power-regions-fordern-mehr-mitsprache-und-beteiligung-europaminister-beisswenger-auch-starke-standorte-unterliegen-transformationsprozessen/" target="_self">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/bericht-aus-der-kabinettssitzung-vom-3-maerz-2026/">Zum Bericht aus der Kabinettssitzung vom 3. März 2...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="article-date">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="article-date"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="count-subtitle">                                                Eu...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="count-subtitle"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="count-text">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="count-text"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="media-date">07.03.2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="media-date"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev"]`

- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**

- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://de-de.facebook.com/bayern/" title="die Bayerische Staatskanzlei auf Facebook" target="_blank">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**

- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://de-de.facebook.com/bayern/" title="die Bayerische Staatskanzlei auf Facebook" target="_blank">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link " data-toggle="tab" href="#lightbox-foto">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R12: Links have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r12)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The button does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="btn btn-primary" type="submit" id="suchbutton">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="suchbutton"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a tabindex="1" onclick="javascript:___vrweb_open_hover_popup[0][0](event);return false;" aria-label="Linguatec Voice Reader Player" title="Inhalt der Seite vorlesen lassen" role="button">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="close"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="date-lightbox">24.02.2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="date-lightbox"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 2:**

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

**Failure 1:**

**Failure 2:**

- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child   active" data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R62: Links are visually distinguishable from surrounding text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r62)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link is not distinguishable from the surrounding text
- HTML: `<a href="mailto:ministerpraesident@stk.bayern.de">ministerpraesident@stk.bayern.de</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R68: Accessible name contains the visible label text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r68)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element owns no elements as required by its semantic role
- HTML: `<ul class="download-document">                                                  ...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="download-document"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Porträt: Dr. Markus Söder, MdL</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="des">Geboren am 5. Januar 1967 in Nürnberg, verheiratet...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="des"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="title">1987 - 1991</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="title"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="pdf-file">JPG, 2.38 MB</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="pdf-file"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18">Franz Josef Strauß, Bayerischer Ministerpräsident ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev"]`

### https://bayern.de/staatsregierung/ministerpraesidentenkonferenz/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#DieMPK">                                         Ministerp...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7 show" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Porträt: Dr. Florian Herrmann, MdL</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="des">Geboren am 7. Dezember 1971 in Kelheim, verheirate...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="des"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="title">1978 - 1982</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="title"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="pdf-file">JPG, 666.40 KB</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="pdf-file"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18">Staatsminister Dr. Florian Herrmann, MdL</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- Message: The link is not distinguishable from the surrounding text
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.bayern.de/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/STK_Ehrenamtsleitfaden_2025_BF.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Leitfaden für Vereinsfeiern</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="pdf-file">PDF, 6.90 MB</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="pdf-file"]`

### https://bayern.de/staatsregierung/ministerpraesidenten-und-kabinette-seit-1945/dr-h-c-alfons-goppel/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7 show" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/26_02_02-eBroschuere-EUSALP-Jahresprogramm-2026.pdf" target="_blank">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.bayern.de/staatskanzlei/eusalp_english/">In English: Bavarian Presidency of the EU Strategy...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/PDF.svg" />`
- XPath: `/img`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8 show" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

*... and 5 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R4: Page has a descriptive title](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r4)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `lang` attribute is either missing, empty, or only whitespace
- HTML: `<html lang="">...</html>`
- XPath: `/html`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R62: Links are visually distinguishable from surrounding text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r62)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link is not distinguishable from the surrounding text
- HTML: `<a title="Externer Link: Mit Klick auf diesen Link verlassen Sie die Webseite www.bayern.de" href="https://www.alpine-space.eu/projects/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://www.alpine-space.eu/projects/</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="count-subtitle">                                                St...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="count-subtitle"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18">Eric Beißwenger, MdL,  Bayerischer Staatsminister ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://bayern.de/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><span aria-label="Bild zurueck">‹</span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190561 > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><span aria-label="Bild vor">› </span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190561 > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><span aria-label="Bild zurueck">‹</span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190022-3 > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><span aria-label="Bild vor">› </span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190022-3 > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev"><div class="nav-btn prev-slide-media" aria-label="Vorheriger Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `#press > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div id="news-result" aria-labelledby="emailfeld"></div>`
- XPath: `#news-result`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`

**Failure 2:**

- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 3:**

- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 4:**

- XPath: `li:nth-child(4) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 5:**

- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27">`
- XPath: `.notify-img`

**Failure 4:**

- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><span aria-label="Bild zurueck">‹</span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190658 > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

*... and 11 more failures for this rule*

**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA dialog and alertdialog nodes should have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div class="modal modal-lightbox show" id="modal-fullscreen-xl" tabindex="-1" role="dialog" style="display: block; padding-right: 0px;" aria-modal="true">`
- XPath: `#modal-fullscreen-xl`

- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="/politik/hightech-agenda/"></a>`
- XPath: `.shortlink-introduce > a[href$="hightech-agenda/"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="/bayerischer-raumfahrtgipfel/">`
- XPath: `.image-box-img > a[href="/bayerischer-raumfahrtgipfel/"]`

#### Rule: [presentation-role-conflict](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/presentation-role-conflict?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements marked as presentational should be consistently ignored
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><div class="nav-btn prev-slide-media" aria-label="Vorheriger Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `.media-youtube > .owl-nav > .owl-prev.disabled[role="presentation"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements marked as presentational should be consistently ignored
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><div class="nav-btn next-slide-media" aria-label="Naechster Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `.media-youtube > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="cookie-text">`
- XPath: `.cookie-text`

#### Rule: [tabindex](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/tabindex?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero

- XPath: `#cookie-button`

- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero

- XPath: `li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"]`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<a tabindex="11" href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCoJkv1QaoW4YjmiE9u85Y2w/featured" title="Externer Link: Mit Klick auf diesen Link verlassen Sie die Webseite www.bayern.de" target="_blank">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<a tabindex="11" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/repr%C3%A9sentation-de-l-%C3%A9tat-de-bavi%C3%A8re-%C3%A0-montr%C3%A9al-state-of-bavaria-office-in-montreal/?viewAsMember=true" title="Externer Link: Mit Klick auf diesen Link verlassen Sie die Webseite www.bayern.de" target="_blank">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > a[target="_blank"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<a tabindex="11" class="open-mail">                                         <img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Kontakt.png" class="sidebar-img" title="Kontakt" alt="" width="18" height="18">                                     </a>`

- HTML: `<div class="cookie-text">`
- XPath: `.cookie-text`

### https://bayern.de/staatsregierung/ministerpraesidenten-und-kabinette-seit-1945/dr-hans-ehard/

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div id="news-result" aria-labelledby="emailfeld"></div>`
- XPath: `#news-result`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Youtube.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Instagram.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Linkedin.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(4) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27">`
- XPath: `.notify-img`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="cookie-text">`
- XPath: `.cookie-text`

### https://bayern.de/staatskanzlei/eusalp-2026/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><div class="nav-btn prev-slide-media" aria-label="Vorheriger Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `.counter.section:nth-child(6) > .section-bg-dunkel.pad-t0 > .container > .owl-module.owl-carousel.owl-theme > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><div class="nav-btn next-slide-media" aria-label="Naechster Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `.counter.section:nth-child(6) > .section-bg-dunkel.pad-t0 > .container > .owl-module.owl-carousel.owl-theme > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<div id="news-result" aria-labelledby="emailfeld"></div>`
- XPath: `#news-result`

**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <html> element must have a lang attribute
- HTML: `<html lang="">`
- XPath: `html`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/PDF.svg">`
- XPath: `.list-other-introduc > ul > li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"] > img`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/PDF.svg">`
- XPath: `.list-other-introduc > ul > li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"] > img`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text

*... and 2 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [link-in-text-block](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-in-text-block?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Links must be distinguishable without relying on color
- HTML: `<a title="Externer Link: Mit Klick auf diesen Link verlassen Sie die Webseite www.bayern.de" href="https://www.alpine-space.eu/projects/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://www.alpine-space.eu/projects/</a>`
- XPath: `.nowrap > a[rel="noopener"][target="_blank"]`

#### Rule: [link-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/26_02_02-eBroschuere-EUSALP-Jahresprogramm-2026.pdf" target="_blank"><img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/PDF.svg"></a>`
- XPath: `.list-other-introduc > ul > li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/26_02_20-Kalender-PCY-Events-deutsch.pdf" target="_blank"><img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/PDF.svg"></a>`
- XPath: `.list-other-introduc > ul > li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"]`

#### Rule: [presentation-role-conflict](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/presentation-role-conflict?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements marked as presentational should be consistently ignored
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><div class="nav-btn prev-slide-media" aria-label="Vorheriger Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `.counter.section:nth-child(6) > .section-bg-dunkel.pad-t0 > .container > .owl-module.owl-carousel.owl-theme > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements marked as presentational should be consistently ignored
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><div class="nav-btn next-slide-media" aria-label="Naechster Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `.counter.section:nth-child(6) > .section-bg-dunkel.pad-t0 > .container > .owl-module.owl-carousel.owl-theme > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="cookie-text">`
- XPath: `.cookie-text`
